***affaire.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:affaire.html>affaire</a> (4579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">affare</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <small>[Term?]</small>. Spelling borrowed again from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_French" class="extiw" title="w:Middle French">Middle French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="frm"><a href = vnd.unilang:affaire.html>affaire</a></i>. The sense “sexual affair” <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">affair</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:affaire.html>affaire</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:affaires.html>affaires</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:affaire.html>affairtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">matter</span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">issue</span></li>
<li>political scandal or controversy</li>
<li>sexual affair</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">business</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgaan.html>afgaan</a> (5353)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">afgaen</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gaan.html>gaan</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgaan.html>afgaan</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go off</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to lose face</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to base oneself [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(on)</span></span>], to depend [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(on)</span></span>]</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgestudeerde.html>afgestudeerde</a> (27275)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afstuderen.html>afstuderen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgestudeerde.html>afgestudeerde</a></strong>

<ol><li><span class="use-with-mention">Inflected form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgestudeerd.html>afgestudeerd</a></i></span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgestudeerde.html>afgestudeerde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgestudeerden.html>afgestudeerden</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>graduate</li>
<li>alumnus

***afgeven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgeven.html>afgeven</a> (7705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">avegeven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*abagebaną</i>; equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:geven.html>geven</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgeven.html>afgeven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hand off, hand <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a>, deliver</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give off when <a href = vnd.unilang:touched.html>touched</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to rant, to voice criticism [+ <span><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span>(about)</span></span>]</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belgium" class="extiw" title="w:Belgium">Belgium</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to give up, to forfeit
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opgeven.html>opgeven</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to secrete, to emit</li></ol>

***afgezant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgezant.html>afgezant</a> (16000)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gezant.html>gezant</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. ***afgieten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgieten.html>afgieten</a> (119998)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgieten.html>afgieten</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gieten.html>gieten</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:afgieten.html>afgieten</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strain, to pour off, to pour out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cast, to form by pouring</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">afgieter</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">afgieting</span></li>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haken.html>haken</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:afhangen.html>afhangen</a> (17071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:afhangen.html>afhangen</a></i>, a calque of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">dépendre</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">dēpendeō</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
